They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

‡§§‡§æ‡§¶‡•É‡§∂‡•Ä‡§∞‡•ç‡§µ ‡§Ü‡§™‡§É ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§™‡§®‡§∏‡•ç‡§µ‡§≠‡§æ‡§µ‡§æ‡§É ‡§¶‡•á‡§µ‡•Ä‡§É ‡§¶‡•Ä‡§™‡•ç‡§§‡§ø‡§Æ‡§§‡•Ä‡§É ‡§Æ‡§ß‡•Å‡§Æ‡§§‡•Ä‡§É ‡§Æ‡§ß‡•Å‡§∞‡§∏‡§µ‡§§‡•Ä‡§É ‡§Ö‡§ó‡•É‡§π‡•ç‡§£‡§®‡•ç ‡§¶‡•á‡§µ‡§æ‡§É, ‡§ã‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡•Ä‡§ú‡•ã ‡§µ‡§æ ‡•§ ‡§ä‡§∞‡•ç‡§ú‡§∏‡•ç‡§µ‡§§‡•Ä‡§É ‡§¨‡§≤‡§µ‡§§‡•Ä‡§É ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡§∏‡•Ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ø ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡§∏‡•Ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§•‡§Ç ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡§∏‡•Ç‡§Ø‡•á ‡§Ö‡§≠‡§ø‡§∑‡•á‡§ï‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§•‡§Æ‡•ç ‡§Ö‡§ó‡•É‡§π‡•ç‡§£‡§®‡•ç ‡§ö‡§ø‡§§‡§æ‡§®‡§æ‡§É ‡§ö‡§ø‡§®‡•ç‡§§‡§Ø‡§®‡•ç‡§§‡•Ä‡§É ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡§∏‡•Ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§≠‡§ø‡§®‡§ø‡§∑‡•ç‡§™‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡•ç‡§Ø‡•ç-‡§â‡§™‡§æ‡§Ø-‡§ö‡§ø‡§®‡•ç‡§§‡§æ‡§µ‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§™‡•É‡§§‡§æ‡§É ‡•§ ‡§Ø‡§¶‡•ç‡§µ‡§æ - ‡§∞‡§æ‡§ú‡§∏‡•Ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§Ø ‡§ö‡§ø‡§§‡§æ‡§®‡§æ ‡§¶‡•á‡§µ‡§æ ‡§Ö‡§ó‡•É‡§π‡•ç‡§£‡§®‡•ç ‡•§

‡§ö‡§ø‡§§‡•Ä ‡§∏‡§û‡•ç‡§ö‡•á‡§§‡§®‡•á, ‡§ö‡•Å‡§∞‡§æ‡§¶‡§ø‡§∞‡§®‡•Å‡§¶‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡•á‡§§‡•ç, ‘‡§¨‡§π‡•Å‡§≤‡§Æ‡§®‡•ç‡§Ø‡§§‡•ç‡§∞‡§æ‡§™‡§ø’ ‡§á‡§§‡§ø ‡§£‡§ø‡§≤‡•Å‡§ï‡•ç, ‘‡§¨‡§π‡•Å‡§≤‡§Ç ‡§õ‡§®‡•ç‡§¶‡§∏‡§ø’ ‡§á‡§§‡§ø ‡§∂‡§™‡•ã ‡§≤‡•Å‡§ï‡•ç, ‡§≤‡§∏‡§æ‡§∞‡•ç‡§µ‡§ß‡§æ‡§§‡•Å‡§ï‡§æ‡§®‡•Å‡§¶‡§æ‡§§‡•ç‡§§‡§§‡•ç‡§µ‡•á ‡§ß‡§æ‡§§‡•Å‡§∏‡•ç‡§µ‡§∞‡§É ‡•§

Keith

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

Keith

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

Keith

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

Keith

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;

Keith

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

Keith

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.

Keith

They have taken the waters, divine,
Rich in sweetness, full of strength, caring for the royal consecration;
Whereby they anointed Mitra and Varuna,
Whereby they led Indra beyond his foes.
